window.onerror = function onErrorFunc(msg, url, line, colno, error) {
if(!window.ta || !ta.has('ta.js_error_array.processed')) {
if(typeof js_error_array == 'undefined') {
js_error_array = [];
}
var err = error;
js_error_array[js_error_array.length] = {'msg': msg, 'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'error': err, 'ready_state': document.readyState};
return true;
}
else {
if(window.ta && ta.util && ta.util.error && ta.util.error.record) {
ta.util.error.record(error, 'error post load:: ' + msg, null, {'error_script': url, 'line': line, 'column': colno, 'ready_state': document.readyState});
}
}
};
</script>

           <div class="modules-membercenter-about-me " data-ox-name="modules.membercenter.AboutMe" data-ox-context="MemberCenter_ProfileData, Errors, Member"> 
            <div class="aboutMe profileBox">
             <span class="header">About Me</span> 
             <div class="info">
              <p>Since Nov 2004</p>
              <p>Lives in Panama City, Panama</p>
              <p> 50-64 year old male </p>
              <p>My wife and I have been traveling and living overseas since 1987 and are now settled in Panama City. We have been here since 1997 and run our own businesses. Along with some parters we have bought the old Palo Alto Riverside Inn, renamed it &quot;The Riverside Inn, Boquete&quot; and are open for business, The Rock restaurant is consistently ranked as one of the best restaurants in Chiriqui. My other business is tourism marketing and my wife has a vacation rental business. We offer reservations and marketing support for small hotels at www.selectsmallhotels.com. Vacation rentals are on www.panamapremierrentals.com. More than welcome to email me questions at: andrew@selectsmallhotels.com or check out my blog at: www.panamatravelexpert.com althought I am not able to do much on it right now. </p>
             </div>
